======================
==== makeNominals ====
======================
 supercut =  MinIf$( WH3l_mOSll[], WH3l_mOSll[Iteration$] > 0) > 12             && Alt$(Lepton_pt[0],0)>25             && Alt$(Lepton_pt[1],0)>20             && Alt$(Lepton_pt[2],0)>15             && Alt$(Lepton_pt[3],0)<10             && abs(WH3l_chlll) == 1            
 outputFileName =  rootFiles_AZH_2018_v7/plots_AZH_2018_v7_21.root

  <cuts>
cut =  preselection  ::  1

  <variables>
    variable = events :: 1
      range: (1, 0, 2)
    variable = njet :: ZH3l_njet
      range: (10, 0, 10)
    variable = pt1 :: Lepton_pt[0]
      range: (10, 0.0, 200)
    variable = ptz :: ZH3l_pTZ
      range: (20, 0, 400)
    variable = checkmZ :: ZH3l_checkmZ
      range: (20, 0, 200)
    variable = ptjet0 :: CleanJet_pt[0]
      range: (20, 0, 200)
    variable = ptjet1 :: CleanJet_pt[1]
      range: (20, 0, 200)

  <nuisances>
    nuisance = lumi_Uncorrelated :: lumi_13TeV_2018
      type: lnN
    nuisance = lumi_XYFact :: lumi_13TeV_XYFact
      type: lnN
    nuisance = lumi_LScale :: lumi_13TeV_LSCale
      type: lnN
    nuisance = lumi_CurrCalib :: lumi_13TeV_CurrCalib
      type: lnN
